    34                                                   function automatic LE;
    35                                                       input [63:0] A;
    36                                                       input [63:0] B;
    37                                                       reg [10:0] exp_A, exp_B;
    38                                                       reg [51:0] mant_A, mant_B;
    39                                                       begin
    40              1                      89995                 exp_A = A[62:52];
    41              1                      89995                 exp_B = B[62:52];
    42              1                      89995                 mant_A = A[51:0];
    43              1                      89995                 mant_B = B[51:0];
    44                                               
    45                                                           if (A[63] != B[63])
    46              1                    ***0***                     LE = A[63];  // Different signs: negative is less
    47                                                           else begin
    48                                                               if (exp_A != exp_B) begin
    49              1                      47264                         LE = (exp_A < exp_B) ? 1'b1 : 1'b0;
    50              1                    ***0***                         if (A[63]) LE = ~LE;  // negative numbers
    51                                                               end else begin
    52              1                      42731                         LE = (mant_A <= mant_B) ? 1'b1 : 1'b0;
    53              1                    ***0***                         if (A[63]) LE = ~LE;  // negative numbers
    54                                                               end
    55                                                           end
    56                                                       end
    57                                                   endfunction
